msg:As soon as you enter the lobby, the fragrance of osmanthus fills your nose. The courtyard is also in Chinese garden style. The swimming pool in the middle is very suitable for playing with children~
The room under the osmanthus tree is in warm yellow tones, which makes people feel very comfortable when they enter the door. There is a small balcony, opposite which is the mountain view. Looking from a distance, it seems that you are in a fairyland in the mountains. It is really beautiful~
In the afternoon, the hotel prepared tea and snacks. The tea is Guilin's osmanthus black tea, and the snacks include osmanthus cakes, matcha cakes, mango mousse and fruit plates.
After afternoon tea, we came to the most important part! Experience osmanthus culture and DIY osmanthus cakes~The design of the osmanthus culture experience hall is particularly beautiful, introducing the life experience and meaning of osmanthus from different angles. There are the world's first osmanthus seeds in the experience hall, which is the origin of osmanthus~The most memorable thing is the champion gate that I crossed, and the sound of the shaking bell is still in my ears.
Outside the experience hall, there is a local specialty osmanthus ice cream. The osmanthus flavor is very strong but not too sweet. It is very fresh and beautiful. I really love it!
Next is DIY osmanthus cake. We have eaten osmanthus cake before, but this is the first time we have tried to make it! The osmanthus cake made by ourselves is particularly delicious. Many children also participated in the production. This project is very suitable for bringing children! Not only can children learn more about osmanthus culture and increase their hands-on ability, but they can also taste the osmanthus cake they made themselves~
The Osmanthus Tree Hotel has a children's playground, and many children like to play there. There are duplex rooms, which are especially suitable for a family of three generations or bringing children to live. You can also learn about osmanthus culture knowledge at the Osmanthus Culture Experience Hall~
